Navigator).</p><p data-renderer-start-pos="115"><strong data-renderer-mark="true">What&#x27;s new:</strong></p><ul class="ak-ul" data-indent-level="1"><li><p data-renderer-start-pos="130">Forge custom fields appear as selectable columns in the List View.</p></li><li><p data-renderer-start-pos="200">When a <style data-emotion-css="9z42f9">.css-9z42f9{font-size:0.875em;font-family:'SFMono-Medium','SF Mono',Menlo,Consolas,Courier,monospace;font-weight:normal;background-color:var(--ds--code--bg-color,#F4F5F7);color:#172B4D;border-style:none;border-radius:3px;display:inline;padding:2px data-renderer-mark="true">formatter</code> is defined in your manifest, the List View evaluates and displays the <a class="sc-likbZx rovKY" href="https://developer.atlassian.com/platform/forge/manifest-reference/modules/jira-custom-field/#formatter" title="https://developer.atlassian.com/platform/forge/manifest-reference/modules/jira-custom-field/#formatter" data-renderer-mark="true">formatted</a> value instead of the raw stored value.</p></li></ul><p data-renderer-start-pos="339"><strong data-renderer-mark="true">Limitations:</strong></p><ul class="ak-ul" data-indent-level="1"><li><p data-renderer-start-pos="355">Read-only — Inline editing of Forge custom field values is not available in the List View. Users must open the issue to edit.</p></li><li><p data-renderer-start-pos="484">No Custom UI / UI Kit rendering — The <style data-emotion-css="9z42f9">.css-9z42f9{font-size:0.875em;font-family:'SFMono-Medium','SF Mono','Segoe UI Mono','Roboto Mono','Ubuntu data-renderer-mark="true">view.resource</code> component is not rendered; field values are displayed as text only.</p></li></ul><p data-renderer-start-pos="607"><strong data-renderer-mark="true">Read class="ak-renderer-wrapper sc-eNQAEJ jMQAHh"><div style="display:block;width:100%;position:absolute"></div><div class="sc-bMVAic hAwnoy"><div class="ak-renderer-document"><p data-renderer-start-pos="1">As recently announced in <a class="sc-likbZx rovKY" href="https://community.developer.atlassian.com/t/raising-the-bar-on-marketplace-cloud-app-security-together/98750#p-219238-shortening-vulnerability-fix-timelines-for-marketplace-cloud-apps-9" title="https://community.developer.atlassian.com/t/raising-the-bar-on-marketplace-cloud-app-security-together/98750#p-219238-shortening-vulnerability-fix-timelines-for-marketplace-cloud-apps-9" data-renderer-mark="true"><u data-renderer-mark="true">Raising the bar on Marketplace cloud app security: together</u></a> we are updating the Marketplace Security Bug Fix Policy to shorten vulnerability remediation timelines for Marketplace cloud apps. These changes ensure a higher security standard across our ecosystem.</p><p data-renderer-start-pos="288"><strong data-renderer-mark="true">What’s changing</strong><br/>The remediation Service Level Objectives (SLOs) for <strong data-renderer-mark="true">Marketplace cloud apps</strong> are being shortened. The timelines for <strong data-renderer-mark="true">Data Center apps</strong> remain unchanged.</p><p data-renderer-start-pos="454"><strong data-renderer-mark="true">Updated Cloud App SLOs (Enforceable September 1, 2026):</strong></p><ul class="ak-ul" data-indent-level="1"><li><p data-renderer-start-pos="513">Critical: 10 days</p></li><li><p data-renderer-start-pos="534">High: 4 weeks</p></li><li><p data-renderer-start-pos="551">Medium: 12 weeks</p></li><li><p data-renderer-start-pos="571">Low: 25 weeks</p></li></ul><p data-renderer-start-pos="588"><strong data-renderer-mark="true">Data Center App SLOs (Unchanged):</strong></p><ul class="ak-ul" data-indent-level="1"><li><p data-renderer-start-pos="625">Critical: 12 weeks</p></li><li><p data-renderer-start-pos="647">High: 12 weeks</p></li><li><p data-renderer-start-pos="665">Medium: 12 weeks</p></li><li><p data-renderer-start-pos="685">Low: 25 weeks</p></li></ul><p data-renderer-start-pos="702">Additionally, we have published the <a class="sc-likbZx rovKY" href="https://developer.atlassian.com/platform/marketplace/marketplace-security-enforcement-policy/" title="https://developer.atlassian.com/platform/marketplace/marketplace-security-enforcement-policy/" data-renderer-mark="true">Marketplace Security Enforcement Policy</a>, a consolidated source of truth for marketplace security compliance expectations, including vulnerability management, OAuth compliance, partner verification, bug bounty participation, and incident response.</p><p data-renderer-start-pos="986"><strong data-renderer-mark="true">What you need to do</strong></p><ul class="ak-ul" data-indent-level="1"><li><p data-renderer-start-pos="1009">Review the new timelines: Ensure your internal processes are updated to meet the new cloud app SLOs by <strong data-renderer-mark="true">September 1, 2026</strong>.</p></li><li><p data-renderer-start-pos="1134">Check your tickets: We have corrected an issue where some AMS Data Center tickets incorrectly showed cloud remediation dates. If you believe a ticket still has an incorrect date, please raise an <a class="sc-likbZx rovKY" href="https://ecosystem.atlassian.net/servicedesk/customer/portal/14" title="https://ecosystem.atlassian.net/servicedesk/customer/portal/14" data-renderer-mark="true">ECOHELP ticket</a>.</p></li><li><p data-renderer-start-pos="1348">Watch the policy page: The <a class="sc-likbZx rovKY" href="https://developer.atlassian.com/platform/marketplace/marketplace-security-enforcement-policy/" title="https://developer.atlassian.com/platform/marketplace/marketplace-security-enforcement-policy/" data-renderer-mark="true">Marketplace Security Enforcement Policy</a> is a living document, we recommend &quot;watching&quot; the page for future updates.</p></li></ul></div></div></div></div></div><div class="sc-dRaagA diWSJy"><h2 class="sc-fEUNkw duGuhK">26 May 2026</h2><div class="sc-imABML class="ak-renderer-wrapper sc-eNQAEJ jMQAHh"><div style="display:block;width:100%;position:absolute"></div><div class="sc-bMVAic hAwnoy"><div class="ak-renderer-document"><p data-renderer-start-pos="1">We are adjusting how some JQL features behave to keep search fast and reliable. Queries using functions <style data-emotion-css="9z42f9">.css-9z42f9{font-size:0.875em;font-family:'SFMono-Medium','SF Mono','Segoe UI Mono','Roboto Mono','Ubuntu Mono',Menlo,Consolas,Courier,monospace;font-weight:normal;background-color:var(--ds--code--bg-color,#F4F5F7);color:#172B4D;border-style:none;border-radius:3px;display:inline;padding:2px 0.5ch;white-space:pre-wrap;overflow-wrap:break-word;overflow:auto;-webkit-box-decoration-break:clone;box-decoration-break:clone;}</style><code class="code css-9z42f9" data-renderer-mark="true">membersof()</code> and <style data-emotion-css="9z42f9">.css-9z42f9{font-size:0.875em;font-family:'SFMono-Medium','SF Mono','Segoe UI Mono','Roboto Mono','Ubuntu Mono',Menlo,Consolas,Courier,monospace;font-weight:normal;background-color:var(--ds--code--bg-color,#F4F5F7);color:#172B4D;border-style:none;border-radius:3px;display:inline;padding:2px 0.5ch;white-space:pre-wrap;overflow-wrap:break-word;overflow:auto;-webkit-box-decoration-break:clone;box-decoration-break:clone;}</style><code class="code css-9z42f9" data-renderer-mark="true">aqlFunction()</code> that expand to very large sets will return an error identifying the clause to adjust. For comments, worklogs, and issue history (searches using operators <style data-emotion-css="9z42f9">.css-9z42f9{font-size:0.875em;font-family:'SFMono-Medium','SF Mono','Segoe UI Mono','Roboto data-renderer-start-pos="409">Effective date: <span class="date-lozenger-container"><span class="date-node" data-node-type="date" data-timestamp="1787011200000">Aug 18, 2026</span></span> Group- and asset-based functions that fetch over 10,000 items will not run. data-renderer-mark="true">/rest/api/2/app/field/{fieldIdOrKey}/value</code> - <a class="sc-likbZx rovKY" href="https://developer.atlassian.com/cloud/jira/platform/rest/v2/api-group-issue-custom-field-values--apps-/#api-rest-api-2-app-field-fieldidorkey-value-put" title="https://developer.atlassian.com/cloud/jira/platform/rest/v2/api-group-issue-custom-field-values--apps-/#api-rest-api-2-app-field-fieldidorkey-value-put" data-renderer-mark="true">Update custom field value</a></p></li></ul><p data-renderer-start-pos="262"><strong data-renderer-mark="true">What it does:</strong> When set to <style data-emotion-css="9z42f9">.css-9z42f9{font-size:0.875em;font-family:'SFMono-Medium','SF Mono','Segoe UI Mono','Roboto Mono','Ubuntu Mono',Menlo,Consolas,Courier,monospace;font-weight:normal;background-color:var(--ds--code--bg-color,#F4F5F7);color:#172B4D;border-style:none;border-radius:3px;display:inline;padding:2px 0.5ch;white-space:pre-wrap;overflow-wrap:break-word;overflow:auto;-webkit-box-decoration-break:clone;box-decoration-break:clone;}</style><code class="code css-9z42f9" data-renderer-mark="true">false</code>, this parameter suppresses the generation of app events triggered by the update. Specifically, it prevents <style data-emotion-css="9z42f9">.css-9z42f9{font-size:0.875em;font-family:'SFMono-Medium','SF Mono','Segoe UI Mono','Roboto Mono','Ubuntu Mono',Menlo,Consolas,Courier,monospace;font-weight:normal;background-color:var(--ds--code--bg-color,#F4F5F7);color:#172B4D;border-style:none;border-radius:3px;display:inline;padding:2px 0.5ch;white-space:pre-wrap;overflow-wrap:break-word;overflow:auto;-webkit-box-decoration-break:clone;box-decoration-break:clone;}</style><code class="code css-9z42f9" data-renderer-mark="true">issue updated</code> events from being dispatched to:</p><ul class="ak-ul" data-indent-level="1"><li><p data-renderer-start-pos="451">Forge app event listeners</p></li><li><p data-renderer-start-pos="480">Connect app event listeners</p></li><li><p data-renderer-start-pos="511">OAuth 2.0 app webhooks</p></li><li><p data-renderer-start-pos="537">Admin-configured webhooks (registered via the Jira admin UI)</p></li></ul><p data-renderer-start-pos="601"><strong data-renderer-mark="true">Default behavior:</strong> When omitted or set to <style data-emotion-css="9z42f9">.css-9z42f9{font-size:0.875em;font-family:'SFMono-Medium','SF Mono','Segoe UI Mono','Roboto Mono','Ubuntu Mono',Menlo,Consolas,Courier,monospace;font-weight:normal;background-color:var(--ds--code--bg-color,#F4F5F7);color:#172B4D;border-style:none;border-radius:3px;display:inline;padding:2px 0.5ch;white-space:pre-wrap;overflow-wrap:break-word;overflow:auto;-webkit-box-decoration-break:clone;box-decoration-break:clone;}</style><code class="code css-9z42f9" data-renderer-mark="true">true</code>, all app events are generated as usual.</p></div></div></div><div class="sc-cmjSyW iZUHLR"><div class="sc-sdtwF ehFeaO"><div class="sc-iYUSvU nqvYh"><span class="sc-cTjmhe jexMre"><svg width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"><path d="M0 0H24V24H0V0Z" fill-rule="evenodd"></path><rect x="5" y="5" fZlvel"><div><div class="ak-renderer-wrapper sc-eNQAEJ jMQAHh"><div style="display:block;width:100%;position:absolute"></div><div class="sc-bMVAic hAwnoy"><div class="ak-renderer-document"><ul class="ak-ul" data-indent-level="1"><li><p data-renderer-start-pos="3">Suppressing events means <strong data-renderer-mark="true">no</strong> <style data-emotion-css="9z42f9">.css-9z42f9{font-size:0.875em;font-family:'SFMono-Medium','SF Mono','Segoe UI Mono','Roboto Mono','Ubuntu updated</code> events will be emitted - not only for your app, but for <strong data-renderer-mark="true">all</strong> apps installed in the Jira instance.</p></li><li><p data-renderer-start-pos="145">Other apps may retain <strong data-renderer-mark="true">stale data</strong> for the updated field, which can lead to inconsistent or confusing behavior.</p></li><li><p class="ak-renderer-wrapper sc-eNQAEJ jMQAHh"><div style="display:block;width:100%;position:absolute"></div><div class="sc-bMVAic hAwnoy"><div class="ak-renderer-document"><p data-renderer-start-pos="1">We are removing support in Jira for permission grants that rely on certain non–group-picker custom fields. These grants work by matching a field&#x27;s selected option name to a group name; a pattern that is being deprecated in favor of explicit group‑picker fields.</p><p data-renderer-start-pos="264"><strong data-renderer-mark="true">Effective date:</strong> May 12, 2026</p><p data-renderer-start-pos="294"><strong data-renderer-mark="true">Affected custom field tied to the field types listed above.</p></li></ul></div></div></div></div></div><div class="sc-dRaagA diWSJy"><h2 class="sc-fEUNkw duGuhK">8 May 2026</h2><div class="sc-imABML hVXNdY" data-renderer-start-pos="1">The boolean usages of the <style data-emotion-css="9z42f9">.css-9z42f9{font-size:0.875em;font-family:'SFMono-Medium','SF Mono','Segoe UI Mono','Roboto Mono','Ubuntu data-renderer-mark="true">autoFocus</code> prop have now been removed from <style data-emotion-css="9z42f9">.css-9z42f9{font-size:0.875em;font-family:'SFMono-Medium','SF Mono','Segoe UI Mono','Roboto Mono','Ubuntu Mono',Menlo,Consolas,Courier,monospace;font-weight:normal;background-color:var(--ds--code--bg-color,#F4F5F7);color:#172B4D;border-style:none;border-radius:3px;display:inline;padding:2px 0.5ch;white-space:pre-wrap;overflow-wrap:break-word;overflow:auto;-webkit-box-decoration-break:clone;box-decoration-break:clone;}</style><code class="code css-9z42f9" data-renderer-mark="true">@atlaskit/modal-dialog</code>. The previously default value of <style data-emotion-css="9z42f9">.css-9z42f9{font-size:0.875em;font-family:'SFMono-Medium','SF Mono','Segoe UI Mono','Roboto Mono','Ubuntu Mono',Menlo,Consolas,Courier,monospace;font-weight:normal;background-color:var(--ds--code--bg-color,#F4F5F7);color:#172B4D;border-style:none;border-radius:3px;display:inline;padding:2px 0.5ch;white-space:pre-wrap;overflow-wrap:break-word;overflow:auto;-webkit-box-decoration-break:clone;box-decoration-break:clone;}</style><code class="code css-9z42f9" data-renderer-mark="true">true</code>, which automatically moves focus to the first interactive element within the modal, is now the default with no option to set it to <style data-emotion-css="9z42f9">.css-9z42f9{font-size:0.875em;font-family:'SFMono-Medium','SF Mono','Segoe UI Mono','Roboto Mono','Ubuntu Mono',Menlo,Consolas,Courier,monospace;font-weight:normal;background-color:var(--ds--code--bg-color,#F4F5F7);color:#172B4D;border-style:none;border-radius:3px;display:inline;padding:2px 0.5ch;white-space:pre-wrap;overflow-wrap:break-word;overflow:auto;-webkit-box-decoration-break:clone;box-decoration-break:clone;}</style><code class="code css-9z42f9" data-renderer-mark="true">false</code>. This is to improve accessibility and follow <a class="sc-likbZx rovKY" href="https://www.w3.org/WAI/ARIA/apg/patterns/dialog-modal/#keyboard_interaction" title="https://www.w3.org/WAI/ARIA/apg/patterns/dialog-modal/#keyboard_interaction" data-renderer-mark="true">the WCAG guidelines for focus within a modal dialog</a>.</p><p data-renderer-start-pos="366">Boolean usages of <style data-emotion-css="9z42f9">.css-9z42f9{font-size:0.875em;font-family:'SFMono-Medium','SF Mono','Segoe UI Mono','Roboto Mono','Ubuntu Mono',Menlo,Consolas,Courier,monospace;font-weight:normal;background-color:var(--ds--code--bg-color,#F4F5F7);color:#172B4D;border-style:none;border-radius:3px;display:inline;padding:2px 0.5ch;white-space:pre-wrap;overflow-wrap:break-word;overflow:auto;-webkit-box-decoration-break:clone;box-decoration-break:clone;}</style><code class="code css-9z42f9" data-renderer-mark="true">autoFocus</code> can be removed by running the included codemod. </p></div></div></div></div></div><div class="sc-dRaagA diWSJy"><h2 class="sc-fEUNkw duGuhK">5 May style="max-width:calc(200px - var(--ds-space-100, 8px))" class="css-15u8od2">Deprecation Notice</span></span><span> </span> Deprecation of classic API token access for Jira Product Discovery GraphQL class="ak-renderer-wrapper sc-eNQAEJ jMQAHh"><div style="display:block;width:100%;position:absolute"></div><div class="sc-bMVAic hAwnoy"><div class="ak-renderer-document"><p data-renderer-start-pos="1">We’r’e deprecating support for classic (unscoped) API tokens in Jira Product Discovery (JPD) GraphQL queries. In addition, some GraphQL queries will no longer be accessible via API tokens.</p><p data-renderer-start-pos="191"><strong data-renderer-mark="true">What&#x27;s changing</strong>: Starting <span class="date-lozenger-container"><span class="date-node" data-node-type="date" data-timestamp="1793491200000">Nov 1, 2026</span></span>, all JPD GraphQL query operations currently accessible via classic API tokens will require fine-grained scoped tokens instead. After this date, requests using classic tokens will be rejected with an authentication error. </p><p data-renderer-start-pos="442"><strong data-renderer-mark="true">What you need to do</strong>:</p><ol class="ak-ol" data-indent-level="1"><li><p data-renderer-start-pos="466">Create a new fine-grained API token in your Atlassian account settings.</p></li><li><p data-renderer-start-pos="541">Select the JPD scopes your integration requires.</p></li><li><p data-renderer-start-pos="593">Update your integration to use the new token.</p></li><li><p data-renderer-start-pos="642">Retire your old classic token.</p></li></ol><p data-renderer-start-pos="676"><strong data-renderer-mark="true">Reference</strong>: For more information, see:  <span data-inline-card="true" data-card-url="https://community.atlassian.com/forums/Jira-Product-Discovery-articles/Deprecation-of-classic-API-token-access-for-Jira-Product/ba-p/3228037"><a class="sc-cpmLhU bsMgDr" href="https://community.atlassian.com/forums/Jira-Product-Discovery-articles/Deprecation-of-classic-API-token-access-for-Jira-Product/ba-p/3228037">https://community.atlassian.com/forums/Jira-Product-Discovery-articles/Deprecation-of-classic-API-token-access-for-Jira-Product/ba-p/3228037</a></span> </p></div></div></div><div class="sc-cmjSyW iZUHLR"><div class="sc-sdtwF ehFeaO"><div class="sc-iYUSvU nqvYh"><span class="sc-cTjmhe jexMre"><svg width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none"
